CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION calculate_match_results() 
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$ 
BEGIN
    -- Avoid division by zero errors
    IF NEW.T1_Overs > 0 THEN
        NEW.T1_runrate := NEW.T1_run / NEW.T1_Overs;
    ELSE
        NEW.T1_runrate := 0;
    END IF;

    IF NEW.T2_Overs > 0 THEN
        NEW.T2_runrate := NEW.T2_run / NEW.T2_Overs;
    ELSE
        NEW.T2_runrate := 0;
    END IF;

    -- Calculate Net Run Rate
    NEW.T1_Net_RunRate := NEW.T1_runrate - NEW.T2_runrate;
    NEW.T2_Net_RunRate := NEW.T2_runrate - NEW.T1_runrate;

    -- Determine Winner
    IF NEW.T1_run > NEW.T2_run THEN
        NEW.Winner := (SELECT T1 FROM Matches WHERE T1 = NEW.T1 AND T2 = NEW.T2 AND Date = NEW.Date);
    ELSIF NEW.T2_run > NEW.T1_run THEN
        NEW.Winner := (SELECT T2 FROM Matches WHERE T1 = NEW.T1 AND T2 = NEW.T2 AND Date = NEW.Date);
    ELSE
        NEW.Winner := NULL; -- Match tied or result unknown
    END IF;

    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

CREATE  TRIGGER trigger_calculate_match_results
BEFORE INSERT OR UPDATE ON result
FOR EACH ROW
EXECUTE PROCEDURE calculate_match_results();

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION BallP() RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$ 
BEGIN
    
    -- Calculate Economy Rate: Runs given per over bowled
    IF NEW.over > 0 THEN
        NEW.Economy := NEW.Given_run / (FLOOR(NEW.over) + (NEW.over - FLOOR(NEW.over)) * (10.0/6.0));
    ELSE
        NEW.Economy := 0; -- Avoid division by zero
    END IF;

    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

-- Trigger to Automatically Calculate Economy & Year
CREATE TRIGGER trigger_BallP
BEFORE INSERT OR UPDATE ON bowling_performence
FOR EACH ROW
EXECUTE PROCEDURE BallP();

INSERT INTO BOWLING_PERFORMENCE (UID, T1, T2, Date, over, wicket, Given_run) VALUES

SELECT * FROM BOWLING_PERFORMENCE;



CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION BatP() RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$ 
BEGIN
    
    -- Calculate Economy Rate: Runs given per over bowled
    IF NEW.balls > 0 THEN
        NEW.StrikeRate := NEW.run*100 / NEW.Balls;
    ELSE
        NEW.StrikeRate := 0; -- Avoid division by zero
    END IF;

    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

-- Trigger to Automatically Calculate Economy & Year
CREATE TRIGGER trigger_BatP
BEFORE INSERT OR UPDATE ON batting_performence
FOR EACH ROW
EXECUTE PROCEDURE BatP();

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_player_stats() RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    -- Update Total Runs
    UPDATE players
    SET TotalRun = (
        SELECT COALESCE(SUM(Run), 0)
        FROM batting_performence
        WHERE UID = NEW.UID
    )
    WHERE UID = NEW.UID;

    -- Update Total Wickets
    UPDATE players
    SET TotalWicket = (
        SELECT COALESCE(SUM(wicket), 0)
        FROM bowling_performence
        WHERE UID = NEW.UID
    )
    WHERE UID = NEW.UID;

    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

-- For Batting Table
CREATE TRIGGER trg_update_player_stats_batting
AFTER INSERT OR UPDATE OR DELETE ON batting_performence
FOR EACH ROW
EXECUTE PROCEDURE update_player_stats();

-- For Bowling Table
CREATE TRIGGER trg_update_player_stats_bowling
AFTER INSERT OR UPDATE OR DELETE ON bowling_performence
FOR EACH ROW
EXECUTE PROCEDURE update_player_stats();

UPDATE players
SET TotalRun = (
    SELECT COALESCE(SUM(Run), 0)
    FROM batting_performence
    WHERE UID = players.UID
),
TotalWicket = (
    SELECT COALESCE(SUM(wicket), 0)
    FROM bowling_performence
    WHERE UID = players.UID
);

select * from players order by totalwicket desc;
